<h2 id="required-style" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#required-style"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Required style</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">It&#x27;s important to note that the scroll area requires the following styles on the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">ScrollArea.Viewport</code> element to hide
the native scrollbar:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">[</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-scope</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;scroll-area&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">][</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-part</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;viewport&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">] {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  scrollbar-width</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">none</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &amp;::</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">-webkit-scrollbar</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    display: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">none</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>

Anatomy\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"scroll-area\" /\u003e\n\n```tsx\n\u003cScrollArea.Root\u003e\n  \u003cScrollArea.Viewport\u003e\n    \u003cScrollArea.Content /\u003e\n  \u003c/ScrollArea.Viewport\u003e\n  \u003cScrollArea.Scrollbar\u003e\n    \u003cScrollArea.Thumb /\u003e\n  \u003c/ScrollArea.Scrollbar\u003e\n  \u003cScrollArea.Corner /\u003e\n\u003c/ScrollArea.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## Required style\n\nIt's important to note that the scroll area requires the following styles on the `ScrollArea.Viewport` element to hide\nthe native scrollbar:\n\n```css\n[data-scope='scroll-area'][data-part='viewport'] {\n  scrollbar-width: none;\n  \u0026::-webkit-scrollbar {\n    display: none;\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n### Basic\n\nCreate Duis aute irure dolor in reprehenderit in voluptate velit esse cillum dolore eu fugiat nulla\n          pariatur. Excepteur sint occaecat cupidatat non proident, sunt in culpa qui officia deserunt mollit anim id\n          est laborum. Sed ut perspiciatis unde omnis iste natus error sit voluptatem accusantium doloremque laudantium,\n          totam rem aperiam, eaque ipsa quae ab illo inventore veritatis et quasi architecto beatae vitae dicta sunt\n          explicabo. Nemo enim ipsam voluptatem quia voluptas sit aspernatur aut odit aut fugit, sed quia consequuntur\n          magni dolores eos qui ratione voluptatem sequi nesciunt. Neque porro quisquam est, qui dolorem ipsum quia\n          dolor sit amet, consectetur, adipisci velit, sed quia non numquam eius modi tempora incidunt ut labore et\n          dolore magnam aliquam quaerat voluptatem.\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n      \u003c/ScrollArea.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/ScrollArea.Viewport\u003e\n    \u003cScrollArea.Scrollbar :class=\"styles.Scrollbar\"\u003e\n      \u003cScrollArea.Thumb :class=\"styles.Thumb\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/ScrollArea.Scrollbar\u003e\n    \u003cScrollArea.Corner :class=\"styles.Corner\" /\u003e\n  \u003c/ScrollArea.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { ScrollArea } from '@ark-ui/svelte/scroll-area'\n  import styles from 'styles/scroll-area.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cScrollArea.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cScrollArea.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n    \u003cScrollArea.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n      \u003cp class={styles.Paragraph}\u003e\n        Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Sed do eiusmod tempor incididunt ut labore et dolore\n        magna aliqua. Ut enim ad minim veniam, quis nostrud exercitation ullamco laboris nisi ut aliquip ex ea commodo\n        consequat. Duis aute irure dolor in reprehenderit in voluptate velit esse cillum dolore eu fugiat nulla\n        pariatur. Excepteur sint occaecat cupidatat non proident, sunt in culpa qui officia deserunt mollit anim id est\n        laborum. Sed ut perspiciatis unde omnis iste natus error sit voluptatem accusantium doloremque laudantium, totam\n        rem aperiam, eaque ipsa quae ab illo inventore veritatis et quasi architecto beatae vitae dicta sunt explicabo.\n        Nemo enim ipsam voluptatem quia voluptas sit aspernatur aut odit aut fugit, sed quia consequuntur magni dolores\n        eos qui ratione voluptatem sequi nesciunt. Neque porro quisquam est, qui dolorem ipsum quia dolor sit amet,\n        consectetur, adipisci velit, sed quia non numquam eius modi tempora incidunt ut labore et dolore magnam aliquam\n        quaerat voluptatem.\n      \u003c/p\u003e\n    \u003c/ScrollArea.Content\u003e\n  \u003c/ScrollArea.Viewport\u003e\n  \u003cScrollArea.Scrollbar class={styles.Scrollbar}\u003e\n    \u003cScrollArea.Thumb class={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n  \u003c/ScrollArea.Scrollbar\u003e\n  \u003cScrollArea.Corner class={styles.Corner} /\u003e\n\u003c/ScrollArea.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Horizontal\n\nConfigure the scroll area for horizontal scrolling only.\n\n**Example: horizontal**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { ScrollArea } from '@ark-ui/react/scroll-area'\nimport styles from 'styles/scroll-area.module.css'\n\nexport const Horizontal = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cScrollArea.Root className={styles.Root} style={{ height: 'auto' }}\u003e\n    \u003cScrollArea.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n      \u003cScrollArea.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cp className={styles.Paragraph} style={{ width: '50vw' }}\u003e\n          Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit, sed do eiusmod tempor incididunt ut labore et dolore\n          magna aliqua. Ut enim ad minim veniam, quis nostrud exercitation ullamco laboris nisi ut aliquip ex ea commodo\n          consequat. Duis aute irure dolor in reprehenderit in voluptate velit esse cillum dolore eu fugiat nulla\n          pariatur. Excepteur sint occaecat cupidatat non proident, sunt in culpa qui officia deserunt mollit anim id\n          est laborum.\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n      \u003c/ScrollArea.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/ScrollArea.Viewport\u003e\n    \u003cScrollArea.Scrollbar orientation=\"horizontal\" className={styles.Scrollbar}\u003e\n      \u003cScrollArea.Thumb className={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n    \u003c/ScrollArea.Scrollbar\u003e\n    \u003cScrollArea.Corner className={styles.Corner} /\u003e\n  \u003c/ScrollArea.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { ScrollArea } from '@ark-ui/solid/scroll-area'\nimport styles from 'styles/scroll-area.module.css'\n\nexport const Horizontal = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cScrollArea.Root class={styles.Root} style={{ height: 'auto' }}\u003e\n    \u003cScrollArea.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n      \u003cScrollArea.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cp class={styles.Paragraph} style={{ width: '50vw' }}\u003e\n          Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit, sed do eiusmod tempor incididunt ut labore et dolore\n          magna aliqua. Ut enim ad minim veniam, quis nostrud exercitation ullamco laboris nisi ut aliquip ex ea commodo\n          consequat. Duis aute irure dolor in reprehenderit in voluptate velit esse cillum dolore eu fugiat nulla\n          pariatur. Excepteur sint occaecat cupidatat non proident, sunt in culpa qui officia deserunt mollit anim id\n          est laborum.\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n        \u003cp className={styles.Paragraph} style={{ width: '50vw' }}\u003e\n          Sed ut perspiciatis unde omnis iste natus error sit voluptatem accusantium doloremque laudantium, totam rem\n          aperiam, eaque ipsa quae ab illo inventore veritatis et quasi architecto beatae vitae dicta sunt explicabo.\n          Nemo enim ipsam voluptatem quia voluptas sit aspernatur aut odit aut fugit, sed quia consequuntur magni\n          dolores eos qui ratione voluptatem sequi nesciunt.\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n        \u003cp className={styles.Paragraph} style={{ width: '50vw' }}\u003e\n          At vero eos et accusamus et iusto odio dignissimos ducimus qui blanditiis praesentium voluptatum deleniti\n          atque corrupti quos dolores et quas molestias excepturi sint occaecati cupiditate non provident, similique\n          sunt in culpa qui officia deserunt mollitia animi, id est laborum et dolorum fuga.\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n      \u003c/ScrollArea.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/ScrollArea.Viewport\u003e\n    \u003cScrollArea.Scrollbar orientation=\"vertical\" className={styles.Scrollbar}\u003e\n      \u003cScrollArea.Thumb className={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n    \u003c/ScrollArea.Scrollbar\u003e\n    \u003cScrollArea.Scrollbar orientation=\"horizontal\" className={styles.Scrollbar}\u003e\n      \u003cScrollArea.Thumb className={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n    \u003c/ScrollArea.Scrollbar\u003e\n    \u003cScrollArea.Corner className={styles.Corner} /\u003e\n  \u003c/ScrollArea.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { ScrollArea } from '@ark-ui/solid/scroll-area'\nimport styles from Sed do eiusmod tempor incididunt ut labore et dolore\n          magna aliqua. Ut enim ad minim veniam, quis nostrud exercitation ullamco laboris nisi ut aliquip ex ea commodo\n          consequat.\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n        \u003cScrollArea.Root className={styles.Root} style={{ height: '8rem', width: '100%' }}\u003e\n          \u003cScrollArea.Viewport className={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n            \u003cScrollArea.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n              \u003cp className={styles.Paragraph}\u003e\n                This is a nested scroll area. Duis aute irure dolor in reprehenderit in voluptate velit esse cillum\n                dolore eu fugiat nulla pariatur. Excepteur sint occaecat cupidatat non proident, sunt in culpa qui\n                officia deserunt mollit anim id est laborum. Sed ut perspiciatis unde omnis iste natus error sit\n                voluptatem accusantium doloremque laudantium, totam rem aperiam, eaque ipsa quae ab illo inventore\n                veritatis et quasi architecto beatae vitae dicta sunt explicabo.\n              \u003c/p\u003e\n            \u003c/ScrollArea.Content\u003e\n          \u003c/ScrollArea.Viewport\u003e\n          \u003cScrollArea.Scrollbar orientation=\"vertical\" className={styles.Scrollbar}\u003e\n            \u003cScrollArea.Thumb className={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n          \u003c/ScrollArea.Scrollbar\u003e\n          \u003cScrollArea.Corner className={styles.Corner} /\u003e\n        \u003c/ScrollArea.Root\u003e\n      \u003c/ScrollArea.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/ScrollArea.Viewport\u003e\n    \u003cScrollArea.Scrollbar orientation=\"vertical\" className={styles.Scrollbar}\u003e\n      \u003cScrollArea.Thumb className={styles.Thumb} /\u003e\n    \u003c/ScrollArea.Scrollbar\u003e\n    \u003cScrollArea.Corner className={styles.Corner} /\u003e\n  \u003c/ScrollArea.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { ScrollArea } from '@ark-ui/solid/scroll-area'\nimport styles from 'styles/scroll-area.module.css'\n\nexport const Nested = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cScrollArea.Root class={styles.Root} style={{ height: '12rem' }}\u003e\n    \u003cScrollArea.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n      \u003cScrollArea.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cp class={styles.Paragraph}\u003e\n          Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit. Sed do eiusmod tempor incididunt ut labore et dolore\n          magna aliqua. Ut enim ad minim veniam, quis nostrud exercitation ullamco laboris nisi ut aliquip ex ea commodo\n          consequat.\n        \u003c/p\u003e\n        \u003cScrollArea.Root class={styles.Root} style={{ height: '8rem', width: '100%' }}\u003e\n          \u003cScrollArea.Viewport class={styles.Viewport}\u003e\n            \u003cScrollArea.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n              \u003cp class={styles.Paragraph}\u003e\n                This is a nested scroll area.
